  - [Certificates](https://supremequilts.com.au/blogs/blog/certificates): <p>Supreme Quilts are always importing various European Class 1 downs many times during each year. All of these downs are continually monitored by various industry regulators. IDFL (International Down &amp; Feather Laboratory) , IDFB (International Down &amp; Feather Bureau, Downpass, Traumpass etc. These certificates are something we seek upon importation as often as we can, included always for every single import is a Vet Health Certificate which is compulsory for importation by Australian Customs and Quarantine.</p>
<p>Downpass is essentially the certification that of RDS, some suppliers use Downpass others use RDS.</p>
<p>For more information click on the link to Downpass: <a href="http://www.downpass.com/en//" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">www.downpass.com/en//</a></p>
<p>The Downpass certification number for our supplier is DE D 7590001</p>
<p>Our documents do not and never will have sections blocked out or hidden unlike another feather and down factory in Melbourne. We will continually add certificates when needed and will continually oust a misleading manufacturer on this issue. We will continually authorise blog pages on their misleading and deceptive conduct. We make no apologies for this.</p>
<p>A Vet Health Certificate in now only provided upon request to cut down on paper waste.</p>
